# Excalidraw Data
## Text Elements
A particle P, is projected vertically upwards, from horizontal ground, with a speed of 30m/s. At the same instant another particle, P2 is projected vertically upwards from the top of a tower of height 25m, with a speed of 10m/s.
a) find the time for which P1 is higher than the top of the tower.







b) The velocities of the particles at the instant when the particles are at the same height ^PjqvCyqh

2 ^pvyyWMdJ

Vertical Motion:
Assumptions:
    - Particle
    - Pure vertical motion
    - Constant acceleration
    - g = 9.81 or 9.8 m/s ^calAzEy0

A ball is projected vertically upwards and hits the ground at the point of projection 8 seconds later. Find the speed of projection and the greatest height reached by the ball ^KRd3K2Ar

A ball is thrown vertically upwards at 25 m/s at the same time as another is thrown vertically downwards, from the same point, at 25m/s. How far apart are the balls after 2 seconds? ^NEBtnTnG
